<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">2.02</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;31, 2022, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter ended February&#160;28, 2022 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">7.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;31, 2022, the Company is conducting a conference call and webcast beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time regarding its results for the fiscal quarter ended February&#160;28, 2022 and related matters. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the conference call are available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A link to the conference call will be available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">9.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Financial Statements and Exhibits</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibits</span> </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2022 Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Strong Execution with Continued Progress on Strategic Priorities </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Second quarter highlights </I></P>

$1.06 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; continuing operations adjusted** EPS increased 25.9&nbsp;percent to $1.59, up 26.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $33.8&nbsp;billion, up 3.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Second quarter operating income from continuing operations increased to $1.2&nbsp;billion, compared with operating income
of $832&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; adjusted operating income from continuing operations increased to $1.7&nbsp;billion, up 35.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Strategic review of the Boots business in progress, in line with the company&#146;s renewed priorities and strategic
direction, including greater focus on U.S. healthcare </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Strong operational performance </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><I></I>Strong execution across business segments, led by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and
testing, U.S. retail comparable sales up 14.7&nbsp;percent, and Boots UK retail comparable sales up 22.0&nbsp;percent with share gains across all major categories </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">WBA continues to serve local communities to manage the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, with
Walgreens administering over 62.8&nbsp;million vaccines to date, including 11.8&nbsp;million in the second quarter </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Walgreens Health pro forma sales up 128&nbsp;percent compared to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
standalone results, progressing toward long-term targets </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The expanded Transformational Cost Management Program is on track to deliver $3.3&nbsp;billion in annual cost savings by
fiscal 2024 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fiscal 2022 outlook </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Maintaining full year adjusted EPS guidance of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digit growth
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., March&nbsp;31, 2022 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the second quarter of
fiscal 2022, which ended February&nbsp;28, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Second quarter results demonstrated broad-based execution, driving strong comparable sales and robust earnings growth. We continue to make important strides along
our strategic priorities, building a consumer-centric, technology-enabled healthcare enterprise at the center of local communities. VillageMD and Shields are delivering tremendous pro forma sales growth compared to their <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> standalone results, and our Walgreens Health segment is on track toward long-term targets. The strategic review of our Boots business is progressing, and our transformational actions are accelerating
sustainable value creation.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">1 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA second quarter sales from continuing operations increased 3.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $33.8&nbsp;billion,
an increase of 3.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The performance reflects sales growth at Walgreens and in the International segment, and sales contributions from the Walgreens Health segment due to the recent acquisitions and
consolidation of VillageMD and Shields, partly offset by a decline in sales at AllianceRx Walgreens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing operations was
$1.2&nbsp;billion in the second quarter compared to operating income of $832&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations was $1.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of
35.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increases reflect strong adjusted gross profit growth across both pharmacy and retail in the United States and a continued rebound in International segment sales and profitability, partly offset by
growth investments in Walgreens Health. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from continuing operations were $883&nbsp;million in the second quarter compared to $922&nbsp;million in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting robust operating performance offset by the company&#146;s equity investments, including the lapping of a gain on the partial sale of the company&#146;s equity method investment in Option
Care Health in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased 25.8&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion, up 26.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing operations in the second quarter was $1.02 compared to EPS of $1.06 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $1.59, an increase of 25.9&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and an increase of 26.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.1&nbsp;billion in the second quarter and free cash flow was $669&nbsp;million, a $431&nbsp;million decrease in free
cash flow compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter primarily driven by phasing of working capital, repayment of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related government support, and increased capital
expenditures in growth initiatives, including rollout of new automated microfulfillment centers and the VillageMD footprint expansion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2022 <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sales from continuing operations in the first six months of
fiscal 2022 were $67.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.4&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago, and an increase of 5.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong comparable sales growth at Walgreens and in the International
segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing operations in the first six months of fiscal 2022 was $2.5&nbsp;billion compared to $298&nbsp;million in the same period
a year ago. This was partly driven by a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations in the
first six months of the fiscal year was $3.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of 41.8&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago on a reported basis, and up 42.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increases reflect strong adjusted gross
profit growth across both pharmacy and retail in the United States and a continued rebound in International segment sales and profitability, partly offset by growth investments in Walgreens Health. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the first six months of fiscal 2022, net earnings from continuing operations increased $3.9&nbsp;billion compared to the same period a year earlier, to
$4.5&nbsp;billion, reflecting a $2.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain in the first quarter due to the valuation of the company&#146;s previously held minority equity and debt investments in VillageMD and Shields,
and the lapping of a $1.2&nbsp;billion charge, net of tax, from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased
39.0&nbsp;percent in constant currency to $2.8&nbsp;billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">2 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing operations for the first six months of fiscal 2022 increased $4.54 to $5.15, compared to the same
period a year ago. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $3.27, an increase of 38.6&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and an increase of 38.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $2.2&nbsp;billion in the first six months of fiscal 2022, a decrease of $372&nbsp;million from the same period last year,
and free cash flow was $1.3&nbsp;billion, a decrease of $550&nbsp;million from the same period a year ago driven by the decline of the AllianceRx Walgreens business, phasing of working capital and increased capital expenditures in growth
initiatives, including rollout of new automated microfulfillment centers and the VillageMD footprint expansion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">3 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>United States: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The United States segment had second quarter sales of
$27.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 1.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, partly offset by a decline in the AllianceRx Walgreens business. Comparable sales increased 9.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales decreased 3.3&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, negatively impacted by a 910 basis point headwind from the AllianceRx Walgreens business. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 7.3&nbsp;percent in the quarter compared to a year ago, with prescriptions filled increasing by 4.7&nbsp;percent,
including a positive impact of approximately 275 basis points from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter increased 3.9&nbsp;percent to 300&nbsp;million, including immunizations,
adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales increased 14.5&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales increased
14.7&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> comparable retail sales increased 15.7&nbsp;percent, reflecting broad based
growth across all categories. In particular, health and wellness increased 43.3&nbsp;percent aided by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-home</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> tests and cough cold flu, and personal care and
beauty increased 9.7&nbsp;percent and 6.5&nbsp;percent, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 13.8&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted gross profit increased 13.7&nbsp;percent driven by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing and strong retail sales growth. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) increased 4.9&nbsp;percent compared to the year ago quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased 8.3&nbsp;percent,
driven by investments to support <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing revenue growth and labor investments, partly offset by savings from the Transformational Cost Management program. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the second quarter increased 67.9&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter.
Adjusted operating income increased 36.5&nbsp;percent to $1.6&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The International segment had second quarter sales of $5.6&nbsp;billion, an increase of 2.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 4.9&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 7.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting the ongoing recovery in the UK market, despite the trading headwind created by the Omicron variant, with
Boots UK sales growing 15.2&nbsp;percent, and the Germany wholesale business sales up 2.5&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased
3.6&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting stronger demand for pharmacy services. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 22.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, with market share gains across all categories, led by beauty. Footfall improved compared to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, though traffic was still below <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID-19</FONT></FONT> levels, with restrictions to combat the Omicron surge in place for most of the quarter. Boots.com continued to perform well, with digital sales in the second
quarter up 60&nbsp;percent compared to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID-19</FONT></FONT> levels in the second quarter of fiscal 2020. Boots.com accounted for over 15&nbsp;percent of retail sales in the
quarter, compared to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID-19</FONT></FONT> levels of 9&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased
11.8&nbsp;percent compared to the same quarter a year ago, including an adverse currency impact of 3.4&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit increased 15.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong UK growth, notably from higher
retail store transactions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in the quarter increased 6.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to
$1.0&nbsp;billion, including a favorable currency impact of 2.9&nbsp;percent. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased 8.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increase in both SG&amp;A and adjusted SG&amp;A reflects increased investments in labor,
marketing and IT compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">4 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income grew 62.8&nbsp;percent, including an adverse currency impact of 7.4&nbsp;percent, to
$173&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating income grew to $226&nbsp;million, an increase of 60.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Walgreens Health: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company&#146;s Walgreens Health segment, created at
the beginning of fiscal year 2022, is a consumer-centric, technology-enabled healthcare business that engages consumers through a personalized, omni-channel experience across the care journey. Walgreens Health will deliver improved health outcomes
and lower costs for payors and providers by delivering care through owned and partnered assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Walgreens Health segment currently consists of: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">A majority position in VillageMD, a leading, national provider of value-based primary care services; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">A majority position in Shields, a specialty pharmacy integrator and accelerator for hospitals; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The Walgreens Health organically-developed business that contracts with payors and providers to deliver clinical healthcare
services to their members and members&#146; caregivers through both digital and physical channels. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Walgreens Health segment had second
quarter sales of $527&nbsp;million resulting from the acquisition of VillageMD and Shields. On a pro forma basis, compared to their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> standalone results, these businesses grew at combined rate of
128&nbsp;percent in the quarter. Shields grew 63&nbsp;percent, driven by key contract wins, further expansion of existing partnerships, efficient implementation, and strong executional focus. VillageMD grew 145&nbsp;percent, reflecting existing
clinic growth and footprint expansion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit and adjusted gross profit were each $15&nbsp;million, both reflecting results from Shields and VillageMD. Gross
profit and adjusted gross profit were driven by Shields key contract wins in the current quarter, partly offset by growth investments at VillageMD which added 82 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-located</FONT> clinics versus the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Second quarter SG&amp;A was $227&nbsp;million, and adjusted SG&amp;A was $92&nbsp;million reflecting the two
acquisitions, and further acceleration of investments in the Walgreens Health organically-developed business. Operating loss was $212&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating loss was $77&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold a conference call to discuss the second
quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, 2022. The conference call will be simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the
website for 12 months after the call. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">*All references to EPS and net earnings are to diluted EPS and diluted net earnings, in each case attributable to WBA. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">**&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the
appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP measure. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an
integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 13,000 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health
services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA has more than 315,000 team members and a presence in nine countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty Company,
Benavides in Mexico and Ahumada in Chile. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been recognized for
its commitment to operating sustainably: it is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) and was named to the 100 Best Corporate Citizens 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:80pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(WBA-ER)</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency
translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute
for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company does not provide
a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available
without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact
diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the company&#146;s United States and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12
consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for
the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same
as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented
on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">11 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company considers certain metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent
prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented
provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as
a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational cost management charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired
inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments excludes the expected profit margin component from cost
of sales recorded under the business combination accounting principles. Stock based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects difference between fair value based remeasurement of awards and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition
compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting
requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include all charges incurred on certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities, for example, including costs related to integration efforts for successful merger, acquisition and
divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance and stock compensation. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and
complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating
performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen&#146;s recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its
financial statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s United States segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the United States segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be
impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within other income (loss). We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying derivative
instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended February&nbsp;28,2022, the Company finalized the working capital adjustments with
AmerisourceBergen resulting in $38&nbsp;million reduction in this receivable balance. This reduction of $38&nbsp;million is recognized as a charge in the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings, in Other (expense) income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of equity method investment and investment in equity securities includes impairment of certain investments. The
Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business and it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis. Exclusion of such charges enables more
consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Other (expense) income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on business combinations due to the remeasurement of previously held minority equity interests
and debt securities to fair value. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2021, the Company recorded such pretax gains of $2.2&nbsp;billion and $402&nbsp;million for VillageMD and Shields respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">11</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gain on sale of equity method investment. During the three months ended February&nbsp;28, 2021, the
Company recorded a gain of $191&nbsp;million in Other income due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in Option Care Health. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">12</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision (benefit) include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision (benefit) commensurate
with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income tax
provision (benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain equity
method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within post tax
(loss) earnings from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method
investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do
not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
